Zoe service is 100 points ğŸ‘

What's more outrageous is that a waiter came into my room in the afternoon to put things, but he was indifferent to the laundry bag hanging on the door, and did not do anything, and the mattress was not replaced.
Notified the front desk to take remedial measures, and then a dramatic scene began to appear. After waiting for 20 minutes, a male manager came up, first asked about the situation, and then started to call people on the spot. I could clearly hear that the big sister on the other end of the phone was very unwilling to go to work, kept complaining, and then she came up reluctantly, with a face as long as Guan Gong. The male manager coaxed the elder sister to work like coaxing the mother-in-law. At that moment, it felt like we were not in a five-star hotel in the provincial capital, but a family homestay. The male manager coaxed her for a long time but failed, so he had to continue to call someone, and another elder sister came. This one's face was even more pulled, because she had just eaten half of the midnight snack and tasted like leeks. As soon as the two elder sisters met, they started to blame each other. Although I didn't turn on the TV, Rural Love 16 was on stage, and there was no need to apply for membership. The way the guest service center receives guest needs is to send a message in a temporary work WeChat group, and then, there is no more. name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:2 Twin Beds Standard 
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Family
info:6 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted July 16, 2023
msg:The second stop in Hefei wanted to live in the old city and feel the fireworks of this thousand-year-old city, so I chose this hotel.

Location traffic:
The location is quite good. Shuanggang Old Street, Gongchen Street, and Xiaoyaojin Park are all nearby. There are all kinds of snacks around, and they are all old shops that have been open for many years. If it is not popular, the pedestrian street and Evergrande Night Market are also within walking distance. The only downside is that there is no subway nearby.

Serve:
The service is worse than the average five-star hotel, but better than Express.
Room facilities:
The gate is the standard Crowne Plaza style, the one with a gate head, very grand. Although the decoration of the lobby is a bit old, the design is good and the grade is still very high. It's different as soon as you enter the room. The room is very small and far from the usual standard of Crowne Plaza. The decoration of the room is very simple, it is the style of express hotel, and it is very old. The sanitation is fairly clean, but the room is damp and there are mosquitoes in the room. There is no bathtub in the room, other facilities are also very simple, and the spare parts are only at the level of express hotels, and the bathrobes and towels are very old.

swimming pool:
The swimming pool is relatively large and the facilities are okay. Many children learn to swim here, and the water temperature is around 28Â°C. But the facilities in the shower area are very old and some facilities are broken. Slippers were scattered all over the floor.

The location of this hotel is excellent, the facilities are average, although the price is cheap, but the price/performance ratio is not high, and the same price is far lower than that of local brand hotels. Although it is a Crowne Plaza brand, it is also a Crowne Plaza Express Hotel.
